# Issue 23968: Meta Ticket on IntegralLattices / QuadraticFormModules

This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to `IntegralLattice` development.
Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to `ZZ^n`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form `L x L --> ZZ`.

- #27876 improved printing for integral lattices
- #25875 constructor for the genus from a symbol
- #25682 access methods to the genus
- #25684 FGP_module transformation to and from the user defined generators
- #25698 locally automorphous numbers of a genus
- #25776 bug in printing of a genus symbol
- #25888 bugs in equivalence testing of binary quadratic forms
- #25890 wrong results in BinaryQF_reduced_representatives
- #26378 bugs in the mass formula
- #25569 speed up creation of `TorsionQuadraticModules`
- #24890 Tensor product of two lattices
- #24888 Construct a torsion quadratic or bilinear form - from a genus 
- #24889 Enumerate all genera of given signature, determinant and bounded scale of a jordan block.
- #24868 `p`-neighbors
- #24864 bug in `normal_form`
- #24821 `_mul_` for FGP_Modlue_class
- #24859 all_overlattices
- #24858 enumeration of all submodules of `TorsionQuadraticModule`
- #24810 `_mul_` for integral lattices rescaling the basis
- #24818 yet another bug in the genus class
- #24788 Twist of lattice
- #25014 Twist of a `TorsionQuadraticModule`
- #24702 bug: saturation and intersection live in wrong ambient module
- #24571 Orthogonal groups of `TorsionQuadraticModules` 
- #24577 `is_genus` for `TorsionQuadraticModules`
- #24576 Brown invariant of a `TorsionQuadraticModule`
- #24564 Primitive extensions
- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
- #24083 Factory function for `TorsionQuadraticForms`
- #24082 Interaction `TorsionQuadraticModules` vs `Genus` 
- #24036 orthogonal groups for `IntegralLattices`
- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for `TorsionQuadraticModules` 
- #23981 use `_mul_` for the inner_product in `FreeQuadraticModules` 
- #23967: Coercion pushout for `FGP_modules`
- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
- #23955 bug in the Genus class
- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
- #23915 use the `inner_product_matrix` to compare ambient spaces
- #23634 a class for `IntegralLattice`es
- #22720 bug in `annihilator()` for the trivial abelian group
- #23944 `QQ/ZZ`, `QQ/2ZZ` or `QQ/nZZ` as abelian groups. 
- #28611 representative computation for genus symbols
- #28942 Maximal even overlattice 
- #24108 quadratic form from invariants
- #28952 Rational representative for a genus
- #29279 	make doctests of fqf_orthogonal groups independent of the generators
- #27358 Memory leak in sage.groups.matrix_gps.isometries 
- #29609 Compute the Conway mass directly from the genus symbol. 
- #29611 Direct sum for genus symbols 
- #30669 Remove ambiguous conversions for fqf_orthogonal groups 
- #30743 fix warnings and breaking conditions for neighbor method
- #30842 genus representatives

The following tickets are not related directly to `IntegralLattices`
however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:

- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
- #13853 Correct `FreeModule.coordinates()` to match specification 
- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 


CC:  @roed314 @annahaensch

Author: Simon Brandhorst

Status: new

Issue created by migration from https://trac.sagemath.org/ticket/23968

```json
    "body": "Description changed:\n```diff\n--- \n+++ \n@@ -1,3 +1,34 @@\n+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \\`IntegralLattice\\` development.\n+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \\`ZZ^n\\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \\`L x L --> ZZ\\`.\n+\n+-  #23981 use _mul_ for the inner_product in FreeQuadraticModules \n+- #23967: Coercion pushout for FGP_modules\n+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements\n+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules\n+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.\n+- #23955 bug in the Genus class\n+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols\n+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing\n+- #23915 use the \\`inner_product_matrix\\` to compare ambient spaces\n+- #23634 a class for \\`IntegralLattice\\`es\n+- #22720 bug in \\`annihilator()\\` for the trivial abelian group\n+- #23944 \\`QQ/ZZ\\`, \\`QQ/2ZZ\\` or \\`QQ/nZZ\\` as abelian groups. \n+\n+The following tickets are not related directly to IntegralLattices\n+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:\n+\n+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons\n+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules \n+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. \n+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid \n+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification \n+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to \n+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense \n+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors \n+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs \n+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r \n+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices\n+\n \n \n Author: Simon Brandhorst\n```\n",
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,34 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+-  #23981 use _mul_ for the inner_product in FreeQuadraticModules 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for FGP_modules
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to IntegralLattices
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,34 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #23981 use _mul_ for the inner_product in FreeQuadraticModules 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for FGP_modules
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to IntegralLattices
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,35 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24035 Orthogonal/Jordan decomposition for TorsionQuadraticModules 
+- #23981 use _mul_ for the inner_product in FreeQuadraticModules 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for FGP_modules
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to IntegralLattices
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,35 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24035 Orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to IntegralLattices
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,36 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for IntegralLattices 
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to IntegralLattices
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,36 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to IntegralLattices
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,37 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24082 Interaction TorsionQuadraticModules vs Genus 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to IntegralLattices
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

```diff
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`

+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to IntegralLattices

+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,40 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24087 Endomorphism rings and automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct FreeModule.coordinates() to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,40 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24087 Endomorphism rings and automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,41 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,42 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24564 Primitive extensions
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,44 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24577 is_genus for TorsionQuadraticModules
+- #24576 Brown invariant of a TorsionQuadraticModule 
+- #24564 Primitive extensions
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,44 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24577 \`is_genus\` for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`
+- #24576 Brown invariant of a \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24564 Primitive extensions
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers
```

```diff
@@ -1,3 +1,47 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24788 rescaling of lattice
+- #24702 bug: saturation and intersection live in wrong ambient module
+- #24571 Orthogonal groups of \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #24577 \`is_genus\` for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`
+- #24576 Brown invariant of a \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24564 Primitive extensions
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

```diff
@@ -1,3 +1,48 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24818 yet another bug in the genus class
+- #24788 rescaling of lattice
+- #24702 bug: saturation and intersection live in wrong ambient module
+- #24571 Orthogonal groups of \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #24577 \`is_genus\` for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`
+- #24576 Brown invariant of a \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24564 Primitive extensions
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs
```

```diff
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #24810 _mul_ for integral lattices rescaling the basis
+- #24818 yet another bug in the genus class
+- #24788 rescaling of lattice
+- #24702 bug: saturation and intersection live in wrong ambient module
+- #24571 Orthogonal groups of \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`

+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
```

```diff
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

```diff
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,59 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #25569 speed up creation of TorsionQuadraticModules
+- #24890 Tensor product of two lattices
+- #24888 Construct a torsion quadratic or bilinear form - from a genus 
+- #24889 Enumerate all genera of given signature, determinant and bounded scale of a jordan block.
+- #24868 \`p\`-neighbors
+- #24864 bug in \`normal_form\`
+- #24821 \`_mul_\` for FGP_Modlue_class
+- #24859 all_overlattices
+- #24858 enumeration of all submodules of \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24810 \`_mul_\` for integral lattices rescaling the basis
+- #24818 yet another bug in the genus class
+- #24788 Twist of lattice
+- #25014 Twist of a \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24702 bug: saturation and intersection live in wrong ambient module
+- #24571 Orthogonal groups of \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #24577 \`is_genus\` for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`
+- #24576 Brown invariant of a \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24564 Primitive extensions
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

```diff
+- #24564 Primitive extensions
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

```diff
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
```
```diff
+- #27876 improved printing for integral lattices

+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,71 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #27876 improved printing for integral lattices
+- #25875 constructor for the genus from a symbol
+- #25682 access methods to the genus
+- #25684 FGP_module transformation to and from the user defined generators
+- #25698 locally automorphous numbers of a genus
+- #25776 bug in printing of a genus symbol
+- #25888 bugs in equivalence testing of binary quadratic forms
+- #25890 wrong results in BinaryQF_reduced_representatives
+- #26378 bugs in the mass formula
+- #25569 speed up creation of \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`
+- #24890 Tensor product of two lattices
+- #24888 Construct a torsion quadratic or bilinear form - from a genus 
+- #24889 Enumerate all genera of given signature, determinant and bounded scale of a jordan block.
+- #24868 \`p\`-neighbors
+- #24864 bug in \`normal_form\`
+- #24821 \`_mul_\` for FGP_Modlue_class
+- #24859 all_overlattices
+- #24858 enumeration of all submodules of \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24810 \`_mul_\` for integral lattices rescaling the basis
+- #24818 yet another bug in the genus class
+- #24788 Twist of lattice
+- #25014 Twist of a \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24702 bug: saturation and intersection live in wrong ambient module
+- #24571 Orthogonal groups of \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #24577 \`is_genus\` for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`
+- #24576 Brown invariant of a \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24564 Primitive extensions
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+- #28611 representative computation for genus symbols
+- #28942 Maximal even overlattice 
+- #24108 quadratic form from invariants
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```

Description changed:
```diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,76 @@
+This meta ticket keeps track of all the tickets related to \`IntegralLattice\` development.
+Here a lattice is a ZZ-Module L isomorphic to \`ZZ^n\`, equipped with a non-degenerate, symmetric bilinear form \`L x L --> ZZ\`.
+
+- #27876 improved printing for integral lattices
+- #25875 constructor for the genus from a symbol
+- #25682 access methods to the genus
+- #25684 FGP_module transformation to and from the user defined generators
+- #25698 locally automorphous numbers of a genus
+- #25776 bug in printing of a genus symbol
+- #25888 bugs in equivalence testing of binary quadratic forms
+- #25890 wrong results in BinaryQF_reduced_representatives
+- #26378 bugs in the mass formula
+- #25569 speed up creation of \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`
+- #24890 Tensor product of two lattices
+- #24888 Construct a torsion quadratic or bilinear form - from a genus 
+- #24889 Enumerate all genera of given signature, determinant and bounded scale of a jordan block.
+- #24868 \`p\`-neighbors
+- #24864 bug in \`normal_form\`
+- #24821 \`_mul_\` for FGP_Modlue_class
+- #24859 all_overlattices
+- #24858 enumeration of all submodules of \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24810 \`_mul_\` for integral lattices rescaling the basis
+- #24818 yet another bug in the genus class
+- #24788 Twist of lattice
+- #25014 Twist of a \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24702 bug: saturation and intersection live in wrong ambient module
+- #24571 Orthogonal groups of \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #24577 \`is_genus\` for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\`
+- #24576 Brown invariant of a \`TorsionQuadraticModule\`
+- #24564 Primitive extensions
+- #24150 Factory function for lattices A,D,E etc.
+- #24521 Abelian groups with gap
+- #24087 Automorphism group of finite (additive) abelian groups. 
+- #24083 Factory function for \`TorsionQuadraticForms\`
+- #24082 Interaction \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` vs \`Genus\` 
+- #24036 orthogonal groups for \`IntegralLattices\`
+- #24035 orthogonal decomposition for \`TorsionQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23981 use \`_mul_\` for the inner_product in \`FreeQuadraticModules\` 
+- #23967: Coercion pushout for \`FGP_modules\`
+- #23576 bug in vector matrix multiplication for free module elements
+- #23699 base class for torsion quadratic modules
+- #23958 allow the inner product to take value in rings different from the base ring.
+- #23955 bug in the Genus class
+- #23916 print a genus using the Conway Sloane symbols
+- #23376 bug in genera equality testing
+- #23915 use the \`inner_product_matrix\` to compare ambient spaces
+- #23634 a class for \`IntegralLattice\`es
+- #22720 bug in \`annihilator()\` for the trivial abelian group
+- #23944 \`QQ/ZZ\`, \`QQ/2ZZ\` or \`QQ/nZZ\` as abelian groups. 
+- #28611 representative computation for genus symbols
+- #28942 Maximal even overlattice 
+- #24108 quadratic form from invariants
+- #28952 Rational representative for a genus
+- #29279 	make doctests of fqf_orthogonal groups independent of the generators
+- #27358 Memory leak in sage.groups.matrix_gps.isometries 
+- #29609 Compute the Conway mass directly from the genus symbol. 
+- #29611 Direct sum for genus symbols 
+
+The following tickets are not related directly to \`IntegralLattices\`
+however they are indirectly as they consider Free(Quadratic)Modules which are more general. Or bugs for Free(Quadratic)Modules that might effect Lattices:
+
+- #11579 Free module equality, comparisons
+- #23978 Rich comparison for Modules 
+- #9576 Allow the operator & for submodule intersections. 
+- #7516 bug in pickling quotient module over pid 
+- #13853 Correct \`FreeModule.coordinates()\` to match specification 
+- #10606 Trouble with deepcopy of vectorspaces where the inner product matrix is specified, see also #10577 might be related to 
+- #14681 dumps doesn't save immutability for Matrix_mod2_dense 
+- #21217 Point lattices (free Z-modules) generated by algebraic real vectors 
+- #16893 Free modules over PIDs 
+- #6452 Submodules of (ZZ/nZZ)^r 
+- #18310 Finite dimensional modules with basis: improved conversions to vectors and matrices
+- #11538 Improve efficiency of fgp_module over integers 
 
 
 Author: Simon Brandhorst
```
